# 分类单词树

## n. 名词

### person 人

#### identity 身份

##### age_gender 年龄性别

- [ ] **man** /mæn/ n. 男人 there were two women and six men on the bus
- [ ] **woman** /ˈwʊmən/ n. 女人 the woman kept house while the man hunted
- [ ] **child** /ʧaɪld/ n. 儿童 she writes books for children
- [ ] **baby** /ˈbeɪbi/ n. 婴儿 the baby began to cry again
- [ ] **boy** /bɔɪ/ n. 男孩 the baby was a boy
- [ ] **girl** /gərl/ n. 女孩 a young lady of 18
- [ ] **adult** /ˈædəlt/ n. 成人: Or certain words or rituals that child and adult go through may do the trick.
- [ ] **kid** /kɪd/ n. 小孩 she writes books for children
- [ ] **lady** /ˈleɪdi/ n. 女士 a nice lady at the library helped me
- [ ] **youth** /juθ/ n. 青年: As he left the bus with his money bag, Robinson added, the largest youth accosted him, a quarrel ensued, and the youth knocked him down.
- [ ] **teenager** /ˈtiˌneɪʤər/ n. 青少年: She came to New York from Detroit as a teenager, but with a `` sponsor''instead of a chaperone.
- [ ] **gentleman** /ˈʤɛnəlmən/ n. 绅士: Propriety was synonymous with ritual observance, the mark of a true gentleman.
- [ ] **adolescent** /ˌædəˈlɛsənt/ n. 青少年: The adolescent experiences identity crises in terms of time perspective vs. time diffusion.

### abstract 抽象概念

#### event 事件

- [ ] **event** /ɪˈvɛnt/ 事件: The election was a major political event.
- [ ] **incident** /ˈɪnsɪdənt/ 事件: The incident was reported to the police.
- [ ] **occurrence** /əˈkɜːrəns/ 发生: Riots are of common occurrence in this region.
- [ ] **phenomenon** /fəˈnɑːmɪnɑːn/ 现象: The phenomenon is not fully understood by scientists.
- [ ] **occasion** /əˈkeɪʒən/ 场合: We met on several occasions.
- [ ] **affair** /əˈfɛr/ 事情: The whole affair was a disaster.
- [ ] **episode** /ˈɛpɪsoʊd/ 片段: The final episode of the series was gripping.
- [ ] **experience** /ɪkˈspɪriəns/ 经历: It was a great learning experience.
- [ ] **adventure** /ædˈvɛnʧər/ 冒险: They set off on a thrilling adventure.
- [ ] **miracle** /ˈmɪrəkəl/ 奇迹: It was a miracle that he survived.
- [ ] **tragedy** /ˈtræʤɪdi/ 悲剧: The tragedy shocked the whole nation.
- [ ] **opportunity** /ˌɑpərˈtunɪti/ 机会: Don't miss this golden opportunity.
- [ ] **coincidence** /koʊˈɪnsɪdəns/ 巧合: What a coincidence to meet you here!
- [ ] **outcome** /ˈaʊtˌkʌm/ 结果: The outcome of the election was surprising.
- [ ] **phenomenon** /fɪˈnɑmɪnɑn/ 现象: natural phenomenon

#### activity 活动

- [ ] **game** /geɪm/ 游戏 you need four people to play this game
- [ ] **exam** /ɪgˈzæm/ 考试 when the test was stolen the professor had to make a new set of questions
- [ ] **race** /reɪs/ 比赛 the race for the presidency
- [ ] **tour** /tʊr/ 旅游 they took an extended tour of Europe
- [ ] **trip** /trɪp/ 旅行 he took a trip to the shopping center
- [ ] **class** /klæs/ 班级 there are two classes of detergents
- [ ] **match** /mæʧ/ 比赛 he always carries matches to light his pipe
- [ ] **movie** /ˈmuvi/ 电影 they went to a movie every Saturday night
- [ ] **party** /ˈpɑrti/ 派对 in 1992 Perot tried to organize a third party at the national level
- [ ] **lesson** /ˈlɛsən/ 课 he took driving lessons
- [ ] **course** /kɔrs/ 课程 he took a course in basket weaving
- [ ] **meeting** /ˈmitɪŋ/ 会议 next year the meeting will be in Chicago
- [ ] **concert** /ˈkɑnsərt/音乐会: The season in San Francisco will open with a special Gala Concert on November 22.
- [ ] **lecture** /ˈlɛkʧər/ 讲座 he attended a lecture on telecommunications
- [ ] **session** /ˈsɛʃən/ 会议 it was the opening session of the legislature
- [ ] **seminar** /ˈsɛməˌnɑr/研讨会: Catholic seminarians attend tutorials and row on the Cherwell with non-Catholic students.
- [ ] **wedding** /ˈwɛdɪŋ/婚礼: They will take a wedding trip later.
- [ ] **journey** /ˈʤərni/旅行: My husband and I, a month ahead of the rush, have just finished a 7-day motor journey of 2809 miles from Tucson, Ariz., to New York City:
- [ ] **ceremony** /ˈsɛrəˌmoʊni/ 典礼 a ceremony commemorating Pearl Harbor
- [ ] **practice** /ˈpræktɪs/ 练习 it is their practice to give annual raises
- [ ] **interview** /ˈɪntərvˌju/ 面试 my interviews with teenagers revealed a weakening of religious bonds
- [ ] **conference** /ˈkɑnfərəns/会议: They count on the aid of the neutral countries attending the Geneva conference to achieve this.
- [ ] **discussion** /dɪˈskəʃən/ 讨论 the book contains an excellent discussion of modal logic
- [ ] **celebration** /ˌsɛləˈbreɪʃən/庆祝: John Di Massimo has been elected president of the 1961 Columbus Day Celebration Committee, it was announced yesterday.
- [ ] **competition** /ˌkɑmpəˈtɪʃən/ 比赛 business competition can be fiendish at times
- [ ] **performance** /pərˈfɔrməns/ 表演 they listened to ten different performances
- [ ] **conversation** /ˌkɑnvərˈseɪʃən/对话: The conversation apparently convinced Mr. Kennedy that the positions of France and Tunisia were not irreconcilable.

#### disaster 灾难

- [ ] **war** /wɔr/ 战争 thousands of people were killed in the war
- [ ] **fire** /faɪər/ 火 they lost everything in the fire
- [ ] **crime** /kraɪm/ 犯罪 a long record of crimes
- [ ] **theft** /θɛft/ 盗窃 the thieving is awful at Kennedy International

- [ ] **funeral** /fˈjunərəl/ 葬礼 hundreds of people attended his funeral
- [ ] **accident** /ˈæksədənt/事故: Victim of the accident was Robert Lee Stansbery, 39.
- [ ] **conflict** /ˈkɑnflɪkt/ 冲突 the harder the conflict the more glorious the triumph
- [ ] **disaster** /dɪˈzæstər/ 灾难 lack of funds has resulted in a catastrophe for our school system
- [ ] **earthquake** /ˈərθkˌweɪk/地震: A tsunami may be started by a sea bottom slide, an earthquake or a volcanic eruption.
- [ ] **revolution** /ˌrɛvəˈluʃən/ 革命 the industrial revolution was also a cultural revolution
- [ ] **catastrophe** /kəˈtæstrəfi/ 灾难 the whole city was affected by the irremediable calamity

- [ ] **qualification** /kˌwɑləfəˈkeɪʃən/ 资格 her qualifications for the job are excellent
- [ ] **identification** /aɪˌdɛntəfəˈkeɪʃən/识别: A religious community with a vital sense of mission achieves a degree of group orientation and group identification seldom found elsewhere.

#### social 社交

- [ ] **quarrel** /kˈwɔrəl/ 争吵 they had a quarrel
- [ ] **apology** /əˈpɑləˌʤi/ 道歉 he wrote a letter of apology to the hostess
- [ ] **argument** /ˈɑrgjəmənt/ 争论 it was a strong argument that his hypothesis was true
- [ ] **broadcast** /ˈbrɔdˌkæst/广播: The description of the car was immediately broadcast throughout Southern Maryland on police radio.
- [ ] **dictation** /dɪkˈteɪʃən/ 听写
- [ ] **reception** /rɪˈsɛpʃən/ 接待 she did not expect the cold reception she received from her superiors
- [ ] **intention** /ˌɪnˈtɛnʧən/ 意图 his intent was to provide a new translation
- [ ] **impression** /ˌɪmˈprɛʃən/ 印象 his impression of her was favorable
- [ ] **invitation** /ˌɪnvɪˈteɪʃən/ 邀请 an invitation to lunch
- [ ] **punishment** /ˈpənɪʃmənt/惩罚: Some families place undue emphasis on food: conversations center on it, and rich delicacies are offered as rewards, withheld as punishment.
- [ ] **conclusion** /kənˈkluʒən/ 结论 a decision unfavorable to the opposition
- [ ] **discussion** /dɪˈskəʃən/ 讨论 the book contains an excellent discussion of modal logic
- [ ] **description** /dɪˈskrɪpʃən/描述: The description of the car was immediately broadcast throughout Southern Maryland on police radio.
- [ ] **appreciation** /əˌpriʃiˈeɪʃən/ 欣赏 he has a good grasp of accounting practices
- [ ] **encouragement** /ɛnˈkərɪʤmənt/鼓励: Georgia Republicans are getting strong encouragement to enter a candidate in the 1962 governor's race, a top official said Wednesday.
- [ ] **discrimination** /dɪˌskrɪməˈneɪʃən/歧视: The report called racial discrimination in employment `` one of the most serious causes of family breakdown, desertion, and ADC dependency''.

#### abstract 抽象

- [ ] **devotion** /dɪˈvoʊʃən/ 奉献 their devotion to each other was beautiful
- [ ] **amusement** /əmˈjuzmənt/娱乐: His appearance as Lizzy evokes not amusement but horror in the audience;;
- [ ] **adaptation** /ˌædəpˈteɪʃən/ 适应 the play is an adaptation of a short novel
- [ ] **adjustment** /əˈʤəstmənt/调整: Hoped-for legislative action on adjustment of the county unit system stands less chance than ever.
- [ ] **liberation** /ˌlɪˌbərˈeɪʃən/解放: If the raw population figures are crucially relevant, then it is idle to think of liberation, as idle as to suppose that Poland might liberate Russia.
- [ ] **motivation** /ˌmoʊtəˈveɪʃən/ 动机 we did not understand his motivation
- [ ] **recreation** /ˌrɛkriˈeɪʃən/ 娱乐 scuba diving is provided as a diversion for tourists
- [ ] **suspension** /səˈspɛnʃən/暂停: They are violating their Charter obligation, the prescribed penalty for which is suspension of membership or expulsion''.
- [ ] **expectation** /ˌɛkspɛkˈteɪʃən/期待: The approval did not arise from an expectation of far-reaching agreements at Vienna.
- [ ] **consideration** /kənˌsɪdərˈeɪʃən/考虑: The Cunard line has under consideration replacing the Queen Mary with a ship smaller than 75,000 tons.
- [ ] **entertainment** /ˌɛnərˈteɪnmənt/娱乐: Cocktails will be served from 6 to 7 p.m., with dinner at 7 and entertainment in the main dining room immediately following.

#### quality 品质

- [ ] **might** /maɪt/力量: The jurors said they realize `` a proportionate distribution of these funds might disable this program in our less populous counties''.
- [ ] **glory** /ˈglɔri/ 荣耀 he valued glory above life itself
- [ ] **honor** /ˈɑnər/ 荣誉 an award for bravery
- [ ] **truth** /truθ/ 真相 at last he knew the truth
- [ ] **speed** /spid/速度: Customary Senate rules were ignored in order to speed approval of the Negro leader as administrator of the housing and home finance agency.
- [ ] **beauty** /ˈbjuti/美丽: It seems to have been chosen exclusively from the winners of beauty contests -- Miss Omsk, Miss Pinsk, Miss Stalingr oops, skip it.
- [ ] **honour** /ˈɑnər/荣誉: Hughes said that he had understood the party was to be in honour of Jerry O'Connor, the proprieter of a Loop gambling house.
- [ ] **wisdom** /ˈwɪzdəm/智慧: But he further said that it was better politics to let others question the wisdom of administration policies first.
- [ ] **benefit** /ˈbɛnəfɪt/利益: Mrs. Henry T. Sulcer of Winnetka, a new board member, will be chairman of publicity for the benefit.
- [ ] **fluency** /ˈfluənsi/ 流利 his eloquence attracted a large congregation
- [ ] **success** /səkˈsɛs/ 成功 let's call heads a success and tails a failure
- [ ] **victory** /ˈvɪktəri/ 胜利 a narrow victory
- [ ] **dignity** /ˈdɪgnəti/ 尊严 it was beneath his dignity to cheat
- [ ] **gravity** /ˈgrævɪti/ 重力 the more remote the body the less the gravity
- [ ] **accuracy** /ˈækjərəsi/ 准确性 he was beginning to doubt the accuracy of his compass
- [ ] **strength** /strɛŋθ/ 力量 fatigue sapped his strength
- [ ] **advantage** /ædˈvæntɪʤ/ 优势 the experience gave him the advantage over me
- [ ] **nutrition** /nuˈtrɪʃən/营养: In this one sentence, he unwittingly revealed the basic philosophy of the nutrition and psychological programs in operation at the school.
- [ ] **competence** /ˈkɑmpətɪns/能力: Some idea of the competence of the women is indicated in the contribution made by them during the past 25 years that totals $840,000.
- [ ] **importance** /ˌɪmˈpɔrtəns/ 重要性 the importance of a well-balanced diet
- [ ] **reputation** /ˌrɛpjəˈteɪʃən/声誉: The women have a reputation for giving parties that are different and are fun and this year's promises to follow in this fine tradition.
- [ ] **millionaire** /ˌmɪljəˈnɛr/百万富翁: Then I made up as a millionaire; but I defended Capital with so much intelligence that a fool could see that I was quite poor.
- [ ] **convenience** /kənˈvinjəns/ 便利 chairs arranged for his own convenience
- [ ] **possibility** /ˌpɑsəˈbɪləˌti/ 可能性 this room has great possibilities
- [ ] **breakthrough** /ˈbreɪkθˌru/突破: The breakthrough;;
- [ ] **disadvantage** /ˌdɪsədˈvænɪʤ/劣势: Though WE have not known him long, he is no stranger in this part of the world; and who has ever spoken to his disadvantage?
- [ ] **intelligence** /ˌɪnˈtɛləʤəns/智力: We, therefore, considered the `` suggestion''an insult to our intelligence, ethics, Bill of Rights, etc..
- [ ] **significance** /sɪgˈnɪfɪkəns/ 意义 do not underestimate the significance of nuclear power

#### concept 观念

- [ ] **mind** /maɪnd/ 头脑 his mind wandered
- [ ] **idea** /aɪˈdiə/ 想法 it was not a good idea
- [ ] **view** /vju/ 观点 consider what follows from the positivist view
- [ ] **sense** /sɛns/ 感觉 a sense of security
- [ ] **taste** /teɪst/ 味道 the candy left him with a bad taste
- [ ] **thought** /θɔt/ 思想 it was not a good idea
- [ ] **meaning** /ˈminɪŋ/ 意义 what is the meaning of this sentence
- [ ] **concept** /ˈkɑnsɛpt/概念: It is ironic that Washington is having to struggle so for a concept that for six years it bypassed as unreasonable.
- [ ] **thinking** /ˈθɪŋkɪŋ/ 思考 thinking always made him frown
- [ ] **attitude** /ˈætəˌtud/ 态度 he had the attitude that work was fun
- [ ] **knowledge** /ˈnɑlɪʤ/知识: This knowledge has come in handy, too.
- [ ] **phenomena** /fəˈnɑmənə/现象: The Taoists were Quietist mystics, who saw an unchanging unity -- the Tao -- underlying all phenomena.
- [ ] **assumption** /əˈsəmpʃən/ 假设 on the assumption that he has been injured we can infer that he will not to play
- [ ] **conscience** /ˈkɑnʃəns/良心: But by 1908 its record of brutality had touched the national conscience.
- [ ] **understanding** /ˌəndərˈstændɪŋ/ 理解 he has virtually no understanding of social cause and effect

#### culture 社会文化

- [ ] **Dept.** /dɪˈpɑːrtmənt/部门: The jotted Lyon: This mad world dept.: Khrush and the Kremlin crowd are confident all right.

- [ ] **dynasty** /ˈdaɪnəsti/王朝: These twin tendencies seem to have reached their height in the Han dynasty.

- [ ] **authority** /əˈθɔrəti/ 权威 he has the authority to issue warrants
- [ ] **department** /dɪˈpɑrtmənt/ 部门 you'll find it in the hardware department
- [ ] **institution** /ˌɪnstɪˈtuʃən/机构: An institutionalized liberalism proved itself fundamentally an institution, and only within those defined limits a license.
- [ ] **nationality** /ˌnæʃəˈnælɪti/ 国籍 immigrants of the same nationality often seek each other out
- [ ] **civilization** /ˌsɪvəlɪˈzeɪʃən/ 文明 the people slowly progressed from barbarism to civilization
- [ ] **administration** /ædˌmɪnɪˈstreɪʃən/行政: This is another of the modifications of policy on Laos that the Kennedy administration has felt compelled to make.

#### problem 问题

- [ ] **problem** /ˈprɑbləm/ 问题 she and her husband are having problems
- [ ] **mess** /mɛs/ 混乱 the house was a mess
- [ ] **risk** /rɪsk/ 风险 drinking alcohol is a health hazard
- [ ] **break** /breɪk/ 打破 the telephone is an annoying interruption
- [ ] **error** /ˈɛrər/ 错误 he made a bad mistake
- [ ] **fault** /fɔlt/ 过错 he made a bad mistake
- [ ] **burden** /ˈbərdən/ 负担 the burden of responsibility
- [ ] **bother** /ˈbɑðər/ 打扰 he didn't want to make a fuss
- [ ] **barrier** /ˈbɛriər/障碍: This recommendation was based on the fact that the hymen was not the only barrier to smooth consummation of the sex act.
- [ ] **dilemma** /dɪˈlɛmə/困境: The first dilemma was the morality of nuclear warfare itself.
- [ ] **failure** /ˈfeɪljər/ 失败 his failure to pass the test
- [ ] **mistake** /mɪˈsteɪk/ 错误 he made a bad mistake
- [ ] **trouble** /ˈtrəbəl/ 麻烦 one trouble after another delayed the job
- [ ] **downside** /ˈdaʊnˌsaɪd/ 缺点 there is a downside even to motherhood
- [ ] **drawback** /ˈdrɔˌbæk/ 缺点 he pointed out all the drawbacks to my plan
- [ ] **pressure** /ˈprɛʃər/ 压力 the compressed gas exerts an increased pressure
- [ ] **difficulty** /ˈdɪfɪˌkəlti/ 困难 I went to a lot of trouble
- [ ] **shortcoming** /ˈʃɔrtˌkəmɪŋ/ 缺点 that interpretation is an unfortunate defect of our lack of information

#### perception 感知

- [ ] **light** /laɪt/ 光 the light was filtered through a soft glass window
- [ ] **voice** /vɔɪs/ 声音 A shrill voice sounded behind us

- [ ] **shadow** /ˈʃæˌdoʊ/影子: Shadow over Washington Square

- [ ] **eyesight** /ˈaɪˌsaɪt/视力: 18: 24 Therefore hath the LORD recompensed me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in his eyesight.
- [ ] **laughter** /ˈlæftər/笑声: Serious, yes, but also much laughter.
- [ ] **sunlight** /ˈsənˌlaɪt/ 阳光 the shingles were weathered by the sun and wind

## v. 动词

### change 变化

#### begin 开始

- [ ] **start** /stɑrt/ 开始 it was off to a good start
- [ ] **begin** /bɪˈgɪn/开始: -- The three leaders of Laos agreed today to begin negotiations tomorrow on forming a coalition government that would unite the war-ridden kingdom.
- [ ] **arise** /əraɪz/ 出现 A new religious movement originated in that country
- [ ] **undertake** /ˈəndərˌteɪk/承担: Doyle cannot undertake to reply to inquiries.

#### end 结束

- [ ] **quit** /kwɪt/ 退出 Quit teasing your little brother
- [ ] **finish** /ˈfɪnɪʃ/ 完成 the boat had a metallic finish
- [ ] **abandon** /əˈbændən/ 放弃 she danced with abandon
- [ ] **achieve** /əˈʧiv/ 实现 she achieved her goal despite setbacks
- [ ] **complete** /kəmˈplit/ 完成 He finished the dishes
- [ ] **postpone** /poʊstˈpoʊn/ 推迟 let's postpone the exam
- [ ] **accomplish** /əˈkɑmplɪʃ/ 完成 carry out a task

#### modify 改变

##### positive 积极

- [ ] **reform** /rɪˈfɔrm/ 改革 justice was for sale before the reform of the law courts
- [ ] **overcome** /ˈoʊvərˌkəm/ 克服 You must overcome all difficulties
- [ ] **accelerate** /ækˈsɛlərˌeɪt/ 加速 The car accelerated

##### negative 消极

- [ ] **rot** /rɑt/腐烂: As an aid in reducing bacterial diarrhea and preventing foot rot, feed not less than 0.1 milligram per pound of body weight daily.
- [ ] **harm** /hɑrm/伤害: It is an irritable rule that does baseball more harm than good, especially at the minor league level.
- [ ] **leak** /lik/ 泄漏 one of the tires developed a leak
- [ ] **abuse** /əˈbjuz/ 滥用 the child showed signs of physical abuse
- [ ] **choke** /ʧoʊk/窒息: Armed with the Nixon opinion, the Senate liberals rounded up their slim majority and prepared to choke off debate on the filibuster battle this week.
- [ ] **drown** /draʊn/ 溺水 I was drowned in work
- [ ] **scold** /skoʊld/责骂: "I shall not scold you.
- [ ] **injure** /ˈɪnʤər/伤害: "Indeed you injure me if you suppose me unconvinced.
- [ ] **starve** /stɑrv/ 挨饿 Let's eat--I'm starving!
- [ ] **boycott** /ˈbɔɪˌkɑt/抵制: Then the boycott would not be secondary, but a primary one.
- [ ] **exploit** /ˌɛkˈsplɔɪt/ 剥削 he performed a great feat
- [ ] **pollute** /pəˈlut/ 污染 The industrial wastes polluted the lake
- [ ] **discourage** /dɪˈskərɪʤ/ 劝阻 We should discourage this practice among our youth

##### transform 转化

- [ ] **change** /ʧeɪnʤ/ 改变 the change was intended to increase sales
- [ ] **turn** /tərn/ 转动 a bend in the road
- [ ] **undo** /ənˈdu/ 撤销 I wish I could undo my actions
- [ ] **adapt** /əˈdæpt/ 适应 Adapt our native cuisine to the available food resources of the new country
- [ ] **become** /bɪˈkəm/ 成为 He became annoyed when he heard the bad news
- [ ] **adjust** /əˈʤəst/ 调整 Adjust the clock, please
- [ ] **affect** /əˈfɛkt/影响: The reduction in expenses will affect employees in the thirteen states in which the B. & O. operates.
- [ ] **digest** /ˈdaɪʤɛst/消化: No possible way for him to digest that jack - knife, and fully incorporate it into his general bodily system.
- [ ] **retell** /riˈtɛl/ 复述 recite a poem
- [ ] **rewind** /ˈriwaɪnd/ 倒带
- [ ] **switch** /swɪʧ/切换: If the lever is pulled to clear a signal or move a switch, the tappet moves a short distance lengthwise at the same time.
- [ ] **update** /ˈəpˌdeɪt/更新: The company said it was the first complete update in 25 years.
- [ ] **clarify** /ˈklɛrəˌfaɪ/ 澄清 clarify the mystery surrounding her death
- [ ] **rebuild** /riˈbɪld/ 重建 The house was rebuild after it was hit by a bomb
- [ ] **refresh** /rɪˈfrɛʃ/ 刷新 I reviewed the material before the test
- [ ] **replace** /ˌriˈpleɪs/ 替换 He replaced the old razor blade
- [ ] **sharpen** /ˈʃɑrpən/ 削尖 sharpen the knives
- [ ] **simplify** /ˈsɪmpləˌfaɪ/ 简化 We had to simplify the instructions
- [ ] **transform** /ˈtrænsfɔrm/转变: A fourth view is the transformation of emotion, as in Housman's fine phrase on the arts: they `` transform and beautify our inner nature''.

##### transfer 转移

- [ ] **fill** /fɪl/ 填充 he ate his fill of potatoes
- [ ] **link** /lɪŋk/连接: Never forget that a chain is only as strong as its weakest link.
- [ ] **pack** /pæk/ 打包 a battalion of ants
- [ ] **attach** /əˈtæʧ/附着: `` Hang this around your neck or attach it to other parts of your anatomy, and its rays will cure any disease you have'', said the company.
- [ ] **divide** /dɪˈvaɪd/分开: Determine the ratio of 50% to the average per capita income of the U. S. ( Divide 50 by the result obtained in item 2 above.
- [ ] **export** /ˈɛkspɔrt/出口: They export also.
- [ ] **import** /ˌɪmˈpɔrt/进口: Jean Fardulli's Blue Angel is the first top local club to import that crazy new dance, the Twist.
- [ ] **spread** /sprɛd/传播: There was reason to believe that Premier Khrushchev was also concerned about a possible spread of nuclear weapons, particularly to Communist China.
- [ ] **circulate** /ˈsərkjəˌleɪt/ 循环 the rumor spread

##### phase_change 物态变化

- [ ] **cure** /kjʊr/治愈: Chairman Khrushchev ( Kennedy ) rattles his rockets ( sabre ) in order to cure his internal ills and to strengthen his negotiating position.
- [ ] **burst** /bərst/ 爆裂 the explosion of the firecrackers awoke the children
- [ ] **freeze** /friz/冻结: In another day or two perhaps; this extreme mildness can hardly last longer -- nay, perhaps it may freeze tonight!"
- [ ] **absorb** /əbˈzɔrb/ 吸收 The liquids, light, and gases absorb
- [ ] **preserve** /prɪˈzərv/ 保存 medicine is no longer a male preserve

##### light_sound 光声

- [ ] **zoom** /zum/缩放: For this reason, he says, the density of the universe always remains the same even though the galaxies are zooming away in all directions.
- [ ] **flash** /flæʃ/闪光: `` I'd just turned on the ignition when there was a big flash and I was lying on the driveway'', he said.
- [ ] **shine** /ʃaɪn/闪耀: A shine in her eyes suddenly became tears and she turned back to her husband again.
- [ ] **clone** /kloʊn/克隆: About 7, 000 acres are planted with the high yielding RIC 103 variety, the clone afflicted by corynespora.

#### action 行为

##### social 社交

##### emotion 情感

- [ ] **like** /laɪk/ 喜欢 (= find pleasant)

- [ ] **hate** /heɪt/ 恨 (= dislike strongly)

- [ ] **annoy** /əˈnɔɪ/ 惹恼 (= make someone angry)
- [ ] **cheer** /ʧɪr/欢呼 (= shout with joy)
- [ ] **scare** /skɛr/ 惊吓 (= make afraid)
- [ ] **impress** /ˌɪmˈprɛs/ 给...印象 (= make someone admire you)
- [ ] **terrify** /ˈtɛrəˌfaɪ/恐吓 (= make very afraid)
- [ ] **embarrass** /ɪmˈbɛrəs/尴尬 (= make someone feel uncomfortable)
- [ ] **disappoint** /ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪnt/ 使失望 (= fail to meet hopes)

##### business 商务

- [ ] **hire** /haɪr/ 雇佣 (= give someone a job)
- [ ] **employ** /ɪmˈplɔɪ/ 雇用 (= pay someone to work)
- [ ] **manage** /ˈmænɪʤ/ 管理 (= be in charge of)
- [ ] **promote** /prəˈmoʊt/ 晋升 (= give a higher position)
- [ ] **resign** /rɪˈzaɪn/ 辞职 (= leave a job)
- [ ] **retire** /ˌriˈtaɪər/ 退休 (= stop working at an age)
- [ ] **appoint** /əˈpɔɪnt/ 任命 (= choose for a position)
- [ ] **owe** /oʊ/欠 (= need to pay)
- [ ] **afford** /əˈfɔrd/ 负担得起 (= have enough money)
- [ ] **charge** /ʧɑrʤ/ 收费 (= ask for payment)
- [ ] **bid** /bɪd/出价 (= offer to pay)

- [ ] **press** /prɛs/ 按 (= push down on)

###### create 创作

- [ ] **draw** /drɔ/画: On Monday, the Hughes concern was formally declared bankrupt after its directors indicated they could not draw up a plan for reorganization.
- [ ] **carve** /kɑrv/ 雕刻 Carve a flower from the ice
- [ ] **tick** /tɪk/ 打勾 he counted the ticks of the clock
- [ ] **record** /ˈrɛkərd/ 记录 the film provided a valuable record of stage techniques
- [ ] **click** /klɪk/点击: Casey heard the click of the distant receiver before he could open his mouth, and it took him no more than three seconds to make his decision.

###### transform 变换

- [ ] **mix** /mɪks/混合: But when the sounds of the two speakers are allowed to mix, there is excellent depth and dimension to the music.
- [ ] **spin** /spɪn/旋转: A single measurement of the spin - spin relaxation time Af was obtained at 10 Mc/sec by pulse methods.
- [ ] **twist** /twɪst/ 扭转 events suddenly took an awkward turn
- [ ] **dip** /dɪp/ 浸 there was a dip in the road

### mental 心理

- [ ] **appreciate** /əˈpriʃiˌeɪt/感激: `` I like his clothes for their drama and simplicity and appreciate the great impact he has on fashion''.

#### cognitive 认知思考

##### reason 推理

- [ ] **think** /θɪŋk/ 思考
- [ ] **believe** /bɪˈliv/ 相信（=trust）
- [ ] **reckon** /ˈrɛkən/ 认为（=think）

###### ability 能力

- [ ] **cold** /koʊld/ 冷的 will they never find a cure for the common cold?
- [ ] **mild** /maɪld/ 温和的 a mild winter storm
- [ ] **freezing** /ˈfrizɪŋ/严寒的: There is a trend to packaging meat at a central source, freezing it, and shipping it to outlying stores, where meat cutters will not be required.

#### domain 领域

- [ ] **oral** /ˈɔrəl/口头的: Folklore is individually created art that a homogeneous group of people preserve, vary and recreate through oral transmission.

- [ ] **legal** /ˈligəl/合法的: He said evidence was obtained `` in violation of the legal rights of citizens''.
- [ ] **local** /ˈloʊkəl/ 当地的 the local seemed to take forever to get to New York
- [ ] **royal** /rɔɪəl/皇家的: The decision was made in Zurich by Prince Boun Oum, Premier of the pro-Western royal Government;;
- [ ] **urban** /ˈərbən/ 城市的 urban sociology
- [ ] **public** /ˈpəblɪk/ 公共的 he is a hero in the eyes of the public
- [ ] **social** /ˈsoʊʃəl/社会的: It would be financed by boosting the social security payroll tax by as much as $37 a year for each of the workers now paying such taxes.
- [ ] **spoken** /ˈspoʊkən/ 口语的 She talks a lot of nonsense
- [ ] **facial** /ˈfeɪʃəl/面部的: Man with facial hair: You can only really pull off a Fu Man Chu if you're a cop, a gay porn star, or a pirate.

- [ ] **digital** /ˈdɪʤɪtəl/ 数字的 digital clock
- [ ] **federal** /ˈfɛdərəl/联邦的: The grand jury took a swipe at the State Welfare Department's handling of federal funds granted for child welfare services in foster homes.
- [ ] **foreign** /ˈfɔrən/ 外国的 foreign trade
- [ ] **medical** /ˈmɛdɪkəl/医学的: The President noted that Congress last year passed a law providing grants to states to help pay medical bills of the needy aged.
- [ ] **nuclear** /ˈnukliər/ 核的 nuclear war
- [ ] **academic** /ˌækəˈdɛmɪk/学术的: `` Outside''faculty members want to be considered partners in the academic enterprise and not merely paid employees of a family business.

- [ ] **literary** /ˈlɪtərˌɛri/ 文学的 literary criticism
- [ ] **official** /əˈfɪʃəl/官方的: Georgia Republicans are getting strong encouragement to enter a candidate in the 1962 governor's race, a top official said Wednesday.

- [ ] **physical** /ˈfɪzɪkəl/ 身体的 physical exercise
- [ ] **political** /pəˈlɪtɪkəl/ 政治的 calling a meeting is a political act in itself

- [ ] **religious** /rɪˈlɪʤəs/宗教的: About half of all Peace Corps projects assigned to voluntary agencies will be carried out by religious groups, according to an official of the corps.
- [ ] **technical** /ˈtɛknɪkəl/技术的: Fiedler was then technical director of Hitler's super-secret `` Reichenberg project'', which remained unknown to the Allies until after the war.
- [ ] **commercial** /kəˈmərʃəl/商业的: The new promotion manager has been employed by the company since January, 1946, as a commercial artist in the advertising department.

### quality 性质

#### importance 重要性

- [ ] **westwards** /ˈwɛstwərdz/向西: The great `` sea to the westwards''was a dead end.

### degree 程度

#### high 高程度

- [ ] **so** /soʊ/ 如此
- [ ] **very** /ˈvɛri/ 非常
- [ ] **quite** /kwaɪt/ 相当
- [ ] **such** /səʧ/ 如此
- [ ] **fairly** /ˈfɛrli/ 相当
- [ ] **pretty** /ˈprɪti/ 相当
- [ ] **extremely** /ɪkˈstrimli/ 极其
- [ ] **especially** /əˈspɛʃəli/ 尤其
- [ ] **absolutely** /ˌæbsəˈlutli/ 绝对地（=completely）
- [ ] **definitely** /ˈdɛfənɪtli/ 肯定地（=certainly）
- [ ] **totally** /ˈtoʊtəli/ 完全地（=completely）
- [ ] **completely** /kəmˈplitli/ 完全地
- [ ] **entirely** /ɪnˈtaɪərli/ 完全地（=completely）
- [ ] **highly** /ˈhaɪli/ 高度地（=very）
- [ ] **strongly** /ˈstrɔŋli/ 强烈地（=very much）

#### low 低程度

- [ ] **hardly** /ˈhɑrdli/ 几乎不
- [ ] **merely** /ˈmɪrli/ 仅仅（=only）
- [ ] **partly** /ˈpɑrtli/ 部分地（=not completely）
- [ ] **slightly** /sˈlaɪtli/ 轻微地（=a little）
- [ ] **barely** /ˈbɛrli/ 几乎不（=hardly）
- [ ] **scarcely** /ˈskɛrsli/ 几乎不（=hardly）

#### relative 相对程度

- [ ] **most** /moʊst/ 最多
- [ ] **more** /mɔr/ 更多
- [ ] **less** /lɛs/ 更少
- [ ] **least** /list/ 最少
- [ ] **farther** /ˈfɑrðər/ 更远
- [ ] **further** /ˈfərðər/ 进一步
- [ ] **relatively** /ˈrɛlətɪvli/ 相对地（=comparatively）

#### approximate 近似程度

- [ ] **about** /əˈbaʊt/ 大约
- [ ] **almost** /ˈɔlˌmoʊst/ 几乎
- [ ] **nearly** /ˈnɪrli/ 几乎（=almost）
- [ ] **enough** /ɪˈnəf/ 足够
- [ ] **altogether** /ˌɔltəˈgɛðər/ 总共（=in total）
- [ ] **approximately** /əˈprɑksəmətli/ 大约（=about）
- [ ] **roughly** /ˈrəfli/ 大致（=about）
- [ ] **basically** /ˈbeɪsɪkli/ 基本上（=mostly）

#### limit 限定

- [ ] **just** /ʤɪst/ 刚刚
- [ ] **only** /ˈoʊnli/ 只有
- [ ] **exactly** /ɪgˈzæktli/ 精确地
- [ ] **precisely** /prɪˈsaɪsli/ 精确地（=exactly）
- [ ] **simply** /ˈsɪmpli/ 仅仅（=just）

### manner 方式

- [ ] **well** /wɛl/好地: Sen. Charles W. Sandman, R-Cape May, said today Jones will run well ahead of his GOP opponents for the gubernatorial nomination.
- [ ] **even** /ˈivɪn/ 甚至 he enjoyed the evening light across the lake
- [ ] **right** /raɪt/ 正确地 they are endowed by their Creator with certain unalienable Rights
- [ ] **hard** /hɑrd/ 努力地 a difficult task
- [ ] **fast** /fæst/快: Then Throneberry rapped into a fast double play.
- [ ] **far** /fɑr/ 远 in 1999 ALIR guerrillas kidnapped and killed eight foreign tourists
- [ ] **else** /ɛls/其他: But Palmer knew, as did everybody else at Augusta, that his streak was about to be broken.
- [ ] **alone** /əˈloʊn/ 独自 could be alone in a crowded room
- [ ] **apart** /əˈpɑrt/ 分离 existed over the centuries as a world apart
- [ ] **aside** /əˈsaɪd/在旁边: These were the last two days set aside by the board for hearing appeals.
- [ ] **aloud** /əˈlaʊd/ 大声地 please read the passage aloud
- [ ] **badly** /ˈbædli/ 糟糕地 fingers so badly frozen they had to be amputated
- [ ] **please** /pliz/ 请 These colors please the senses
- [ ] **safely** /ˈseɪfli/ 安全地 we are safely out of there
- [ ] **forever** /fərˈɛvər/ 永远 no one can live forever
- [ ] **shortly** /ˈʃɔrtli/ 不久 he was at the airport shortly before she was expected to arrive
- [ ] **somehow** /ˈsəmˌhaʊ/ 以某种方式 they managed somehow
- [ ] **together** /təˈgɛðər/ 一起 she's really together
- [ ] **properly** /ˈprɑpərli/ 适当地 please do your job properly!
- [ ] **sincerely** /sɪnˈsɪrli/ 真诚地 she praised him sincerely for his victory
- [ ] **personally** /ˈpərsənəli/ 个人地 speaking personally, I would not want to go
- [ ] **regardless** /rəˈgɑrdləs/ 不管 careless of the consequences
- [ ] **deliberately** /dɪˈlɪbərətli/ 故意地 he used that word intentionally

### mood 语气

- [ ] **really** /ˈrɪli/ 真正地 she was now truly American
- [ ] **certainly** /ˈsərtənli/ 当然 the results are surely encouraging
- [ ] **maybe** /ˈmeɪbi/ 也许 perhaps she will call tomorrow
- [ ] **perhaps** /pərˈhæps/ 也许 perhaps she will call tomorrow
- [ ] **probably** /ˈprɑbəˌbli/ 可能 He is probably out of the country
- [ ] **yes** /jɛs/ 是的 I was hoping for a yes
- [ ] **truly** /ˈtruli/ 真实地 she was now truly American
- [ ] **indeed** /ˌɪnˈdid/ 确实 they said the car would break down and indeed it did
- [ ] **actually** /ˈæˌkʧuəli/ 实际上 to be nominally but not actually independent
- [ ] **possibly** /ˈpɑsəbli/ 可能 perhaps she will call tomorrow
- [ ] **generally** /ˈʤɛnərəli/ 通常 by and large it doesn't rain much here
- [ ] **fortunately** /ˈfɔrʧənətli/ 幸运地 fortunately the weather was good
- [ ] **unfortunately** /ənˈfɔrʧənətli/ 不幸地 unfortunately it rained all day

### conjunct 连接

- [ ] **then** /ðɛn/ 然后 we will arrive before then
- [ ] **also** /ˈɔlsoʊ/ 也 he has a Mercedes, too
- [ ] **next** /nɛkst/ 下一个 the following day
- [ ] **still** /stɪl/ 仍然 he wanted some stills for a magazine ad
- [ ] **too** /tu/ 也 too big
- [ ] **rather** /ˈrəðər/ 相当 rather than disappoint the children, he did two quick tricks before he left
- [ ] **yet** /jɛt/ 然而 I have yet to see the results
- [ ] **although** /ˌɔlˈðoʊ/虽然: A House committee which heard his local option proposal is expected to give it a favorable report, although the resolution faces hard sledding later.
- [ ] **though** /ðoʊ/ 虽然 it might be unpleasant, though
- [ ] **while** /waɪl/ 当 he was here for a little while
- [ ] **thus** /ðəs/因此: But thus far there has been no response in kind.
- [ ] **anyhow** /ˈɛniˌhaʊ/ 无论如何 Anyhow, he is dead now
- [ ] **anyway** /ˈɛniˌweɪ/ 无论如何 Anyhow, he is dead now
- [ ] **however** /ˌhaʊˈɛvər/ 然而 although I'm a little afraid, however I'd like to try it
- [ ] **besides** /ˌbiˈsaɪdz/ 此外 I don't want to go to a restaurant; besides, we can't afford it
- [ ] **instead** /ˌɪnˈstɛd/ 代替 Felix became a herpetologist instead
- [ ] **meanwhile** /ˈminˌwaɪl/ 同时 meanwhile the socialists are running the government
- [ ] **otherwise** /ˈəðərˌwaɪz/ 否则 the outcome was otherwise
- [ ] **therefore** /ˈðɛrˌfɔr/ 因此 therefore X must be true
- [ ] **eventually** /ɪˈvɛnʧəwəli/最终: The Federal program eventually should have a favorable impact on Missouri's depressed areas, and in the long run that will benefit St. Louis as well.

## prep. 介词

### time 时间

- [ ] **in** /ɪn/ 在...里
- [ ] **on** /ɔn/ 在...上 left the oven on
- [ ] **at** /æt/在: The grand jury took a swipe at the State Welfare Department's handling of federal funds granted for child welfare services in foster homes.
- [ ] **during** /ˈdʊrɪŋ/ 在...期间
- [ ] **within** /wɪˈθɪn/ 在...之内 inside, the car is a mess
- [ ] **throughout** /θruaʊt/ 贯穿 the play was excellent end-to-end

### place 地点

#### location 位置

- [ ] **in** /ɪn/ 在...里
- [ ] **on** /ɔn/ 在...上 left the oven on
- [ ] **at** /æt/在: The grand jury took a swipe at the State Welfare Department's handling of federal funds granted for child welfare services in foster homes.
- [ ] **over** /ˈoʊvər/ 在...上方
- [ ] **between** /bɪtˈwin/ 在...之间 dancing all the dances with little rest between
- [ ] **under** /ˈəndər/ 在...下面 nether garments
- [ ] **above** /əˈbəv/ 在...上方 for instructions refer to the above
- [ ] **below** /bɪˈloʊ/ 在...下方
- [ ] **among** /əˈməŋ/ 在...之中
- [ ] **behind** /bɪˈhaɪnd/ 在...后面 he deserves a good kick in the butt
- [ ] **beside** /ˌbiˈsaɪd/ 在...旁边
- [ ] **near** /nɪr/ 在...附近 We were approaching our destination
- [ ] **against** /əˈgɛnst/反对: -- State representatives decided Thursday against taking a poll on what kind of taxes Texans would prefer to pay.
- [ ] **upon** /əˈpɑn/ 在...上
- [ ] **beyond** /bɪɔnd/ 超出 through the valley and beyond
- [ ] **beneath** /bɪˈniθ/ 在...下面
- [ ] **opposite** /ˈɑpəzɪt/ 在...对面 to him the antonym of `gay' was `depressed'
- [ ] **alongside** /əˈlɔŋˈsaɪd/ 在...旁边 anchored close aboard another ship

#### direction 方向

- [ ] **to** /tɪ/向: It recommended that Fulton legislators act `` to have these laws studied and revised to the end of modernizing and improving them''.
- [ ] **up** /əp/ 向上 up the ante
- [ ] **into** /ˈɪntu/进入: The resolution, which Barber tossed into the House hopper Friday, will be formally read Monday.
- [ ] **across** /əˈkrɔs/ 穿过 the football field was 300 feet across
- [ ] **down** /daʊn/向下: Each ally will have to carry out obligations long since laid down, but never completely fulfilled.
- [ ] **off** /ɔf/ 离开 The mafia boss ordered his enemies murdered
- [ ] **along** /əˈlɔŋ/ 沿着 we drove along admiring the view
- [ ] **around** /əraʊnd/ 在...周围 a few spectators standing about
- [ ] **past** /pæst/ 经过 forget the past
- [ ] **toward** /təˈwɔrd/向: Gov. Vandiver is expected to make the traditional visit to both chambers as they work toward adjournment.
- [ ] **towards** /təˈwɔrdz/向: We were his Trinity, and he behaved towards us with a mixture of trust and abuse, passion and irritation.
- [ ] **onto** /ˈɔntu/ 到...上
- [ ] **round** /raʊnd/环绕: Bill Jr., 20, Kathy, 15, and Patricia, 9, round out the Shea family.

### manner 方式

- [ ] **in** /ɪn/ 在...里
- [ ] **with** /wɪθ/和: Hartsfield has been mayor of Atlanta, with exception of one brief interlude, since 1937.
- [ ] **by** /baɪ/ 通过 every hour a train goes past
- [ ] **like** /laɪk/ 像 dogs, foxes, and the like
- [ ] **via** /ˈviə/经由: They're contaminating the earth's atmosphere including their own via mighty megaton bombs but their own peasants still don't know about it!!
- [ ] **per** /pər/每: The social security payroll tax is now 6 per cent -- 3 per cent on each worker and employer -- on the first $4,800 of pay per year.

### reason 原因

- [x] **of** /əv/的: The jury said it did find that many of Georgia's registration and election laws `` are outmoded or inadequate and often ambiguous''.
- [x] **from** /frəm/从: Mayor William B. Hartsfield filed suit for divorce from his wife, Pearl Williams Hartsfield, in Fulton Superior Court Friday.
- [x] **through** /θru/ 通过 certain to make history before he's done

### possession 所属

- [ ] **without** /wɪˈθaʊt/没有: Mr. Nixon, for his part, would oppose intervention in Cuba without specific provocation.

### exclusion 排除

- [ ] **plus** /pləs/加: Within view of the avenue are some of the United States government's tremendous buildings, plus shrines and monuments.
- [ ] **minus** /ˈmaɪnəs/ 减 the subtraction of three from four leaves one
- [ ] **except** /ɪkˈsɛpt/ 除了 he demurred at my suggestion to work on Saturday
- [ ] **unlike** /ənˈlaɪk/ 不像 for twins they are very unlike

## conj. 连词

### subordinate 从属

#### time 时间

- [ ] **as soon as** /ɛz sun ɛz/ 一...就
- [ ] **as long as** /ɛz lɔŋ ɛz/只要: It is one that most try to avoid, as long as they can see an alternative approach to the problem.
- [ ] **by the time** /baɪ ðə taɪm/ 到...时
- [ ] **when** /wɪn/当: When the crowd was asked whether it wanted to wait one more term to make the race, it voted no -- and there were no dissents.
- [ ] **after** /ˈæftər/之后: Ordinary Williams said he, too, was subjected to anonymous calls soon after he scheduled the election.
- [ ] **before** /ˌbiˈfɔr/ 之前 I had known her before
- [ ] **once** /wəns/ 一次 once I ran into her
- [ ] **since** /sɪns/自从: Hartsfield has been mayor of Atlanta, with exception of one brief interlude, since 1937.
- [ ] **until** /ənˈtɪl/直到: Noting that Plainfield last year had lost the Mack Truck Co. plant, he said industry will not come into this state until there is tax reform.
- [ ] **while** /waɪl/ 当 he was here for a little while
- [ ] **till** /tɪl/直到: Till seven times??
- [ ] **whenever** /wɛˈnɛvər/无论何时: And whenever the Lo Shu involved directional symbolism, it was oriented in this same fashion.

#### condition 条件

- [ ] **if** /ɪf/如果: `` If you destroy confidence in banks, you do something to the economy'', he said.

- [ ] **unless** /ənˈlɛs/除非: He said `` Morris County is rapidly changing and unless steps are taken to preserve the green areas, there will be no land left to preserve''.
- [ ] **in case** /ɪn keɪs/以防: Mr. Hawksley said he was not critical of city residents for not knowing what to do or where to assemble in case of an air attack.
- [ ] **on condition that** /ɔn kənˈdɪʃən ðət/条件是: "If you take the charge of this key,"continued his mistress,"remember it is upon condition that you never give it out of your own hands.
- [ ] **provided** /prəˈvaɪdɪd/ 假如 We provided the room with an electrical heater

#### reason 原因

- [ ] **because** /bɪˈkəz/因为: The escheat law cannot be enforced now because it is almost impossible to locate such property, Daniel declared.
- [ ] **as** /ɛz/作为: The City Purchasing Department, the jury said, `` is lacking in experienced clerical personnel as a result of city personnel policies''.
- [ ] **since** /sɪns/自从: Hartsfield has been mayor of Atlanta, with exception of one brief interlude, since 1937.
- [ ] **now that** /naʊ ðət/既然: `` I think I can do a better job with the glove, now that I know the hitters around the league a little better'', he said.

#### concession 让步

- [ ] **no matter** /noʊ ˈmætər/无论: He said no matter what stand he takes it would be misconstrued that he was sympathetic to one or the other of the Republicans.
- [ ] **even if** /ˈivɪn ɪf/即使: Nice, even if a trifle gaudy.
- [ ] **even though** /ˈivɪn ðoʊ/即使: They would like to convey the notion something is being done, even though it is something they know to be ineffectual.
- [ ] **although** /ˌɔlˈðoʊ/虽然: A House committee which heard his local option proposal is expected to give it a favorable report, although the resolution faces hard sledding later.
- [ ] **though** /ðoʊ/ 虽然 it might be unpleasant, though
- [ ] **while** /waɪl/ 当 he was here for a little while

#### comparison 比较

- [ ] **than** /ðən/比: The petition said that the couple has not lived together as man and wife for more than a year.

#### place 地点

- [ ] **where** /wɛr/哪里: Mr. Hawksley said he was not critical of city residents for not knowing what to do or where to assemble in case of an air attack.
- [ ] **wherever** /wɛˈrɛvər/无论哪里: They supplemented their income by small government assistance, by tutoring and economizing wherever they could.

#### question 疑问从句

- [ ] **how** /haʊ/如何: He did not say by how much.
- [ ] **whether** /ˈwɛðər/是否: When the crowd was asked whether it wanted to wait one more term to make the race, it voted no -- and there were no dissents.
- [ ] **why** /waɪ/为什么: One Republican senator told this correspondent that he was constantly being asked why he didn't attack the Kennedy administration on this score.

#### manner 方式

- [ ] **as if** /ɛz ɪf/好像: As if to confirm his stature, he quickly won three of the first eight tournaments.
- [ ] **as though** /ɛz ðoʊ/好像: Now, apparently happier under new managers, Mays and Mantle, the perfect players, are behaving as though they're going to pass those previous peaks.

#### purpose 目的结果

- [ ] **in order that** /ɪn ˈɔrdər ðət/为了: If possible, he should make an appointment in order that all persons involved may be present.
- [ ] **so that** /soʊ ðət/以便: Along with a director, the city should provide a CD headquarters so that pertinent information about the local organization would be centralized.

- [ ] **none** /nən/没有: But he added that none of Georgia's congressmen specifically asked him to offer the resolution.
- [ ] **nobody** /ˈnoʊˌbɑˌdi/没有人: `` Nobody really expects to evacuate.
- [ ] **anyone** /ˈɛniˌwən/任何人: `` I find it hard to understand how anyone seeking a position in public life could demonstrate such poor judgment and bad taste.
- [ ] **nothing** /ˈnəθɪŋ/ 没有东西 it looked like nothing I had ever seen before
- [ ] **someone** /ˈsəmˌwən/ 某人 there was too much for one person to do
- [ ] **anybody** /ˈɛnibədi/任何人: So, if anybody solicits by phone, make sure you mail the dough to the above.
- [ ] **everyone** /ˈɛvriˌwən/每个人: It is one of the rare public ventures here on which nearly everyone is agreed.
- [ ] **somebody** /ˈsəmˌbɑdi/ 某人 there was too much for one person to do
- [ ] **anything** /ˈɛniˌθɪŋ/任何事: I told him what Liston had said and he said Liston was a double-crosser and said anything he ( Liston ) got was through a keyhole.
- [ ] **everybody** /ˈɛvriˌbɑdi/每个人: Everybody has a different idea on the ethics and morals of driving away neighbors, when and if.
- [ ] **something** /ˈsəmθɪŋ/某事: `` If you destroy confidence in banks, you do something to the economy'', he said.
- [ ] **everything** /ˈɛvriˌθɪŋ/所有事: `` Everything went real smooth'', the sheriff said.

### relative 关系代词

- [ ] **as** /ɛz/作为: The City Purchasing Department, the jury said, `` is lacking in experienced clerical personnel as a result of city personnel policies''.
- [ ] **who** /hu/谁: Despite the warning, there was a unanimous vote to enter a candidate, according to Republicans who attended.
- [ ] **whom** /hum/谁: The lawyer with whom I studied law steered me off the Socialist track.

### demonstrative 指示代词

- [x] **same** /seɪm/相同的: At the same time reaction among anti-organization Democratic leaders and in the Liberal party to the Mayor's reported plan was generally favorable.

## num. 数词

### cardinal 基数词

- [ ] **one** /wən/ 一 he has the one but will need a two and three to go with it
- [ ] **two** /tu/二: However, the jury said it believes `` these two offices should be combined to achieve greater efficiency and reduce the cost of administration''.
- [ ] **three** /θri/三: He will be succeeded by Rob Ledford of Gainesville, who has been an assistant more than three years.
- [ ] **four** /fɔr/四: Division four will be headed by the Navy, followed by 11 states;;
- [ ] **five** /faɪv/五: Before entering the service, Pfaff for five years did clerical work with a general merchandising and wholesale firm in New Orleans.

- [ ] **nine** /naɪn/九: Mr. Hawksley, the state's general treasurer, has been a part-time CD director in the city for the last nine years.
- [ ] **ten** /tɛn/十: Participating members may attend five of the concerts for $9 ( not all ten concerts as was erroneously announced earlier in The Chronicle ).
- [ ] **eleven** /ˈilɛvən/十一: Eleven dummy rounds were fired by Lauchli in a demonstration of rapid-fire mortar shooting.
- [ ] **twelve** /twɛlv/十二: Arnold Palmer has been a blazing figure in golf over the past twelve months.
- [ ] **thirteen** /ˈθərˈtin/十三: However, this would require a lengthening of the season from thirteen to fourteen weeks.
- [ ] **fifteen** /ˈfɪfˈtin/十五: -- Fifteen members of the Republican State Committee who are retiring -- voluntarily -- this year were honored yesterday by their colleagues.
- [ ] **twenty** /tˈwɛnti/二十: Indonesia is one of the twenty under-developed countries of Asia, Africa and Latin America that are receiving Soviet aid.
- [ ] **thirty** /ˈθərˌdi/三十: The first thirty to sixty days after individuals make their decision will determine their interest and participation in the life of the Church.
- [ ] **forty** /ˈfɔrti/四十: Whose chord is one hundred and sixty feet, and whose vortex is forty feet ( it was actually 37 feet ) above the high-water mark.
- [ ] **fifty** /ˈfɪfti/五十: For example, in a typical store installation, fifty 24-in. and six 36-in. red acrylic letters were mounted against a white painted wood background.
- [ ] **ninety** /ˈnaɪnti/九十: Providing these means are about ninety companies which manufactured the estimated 1,800,000 boat trailers now in use.
- [ ] **hundred** /ˈhənərd/百: In the early spring of 1913 a few hundred thousand persons turned out to watch 5000 women parade.
- [ ] **thousand** /ˈθaʊzənd/千: In the early spring of 1913 a few hundred thousand persons turned out to watch 5000 women parade.
- [ ] **million** /ˈmɪljən/百万: Vandiver likely will mention the $100 million highway bond issue approved earlier in the session as his first priority item.
- [ ] **billion** /ˈbɪljən/十亿: Other parts of the Kennedy health plan would entail federal grants of 750 million to 1 billion dollars over the next 10 years.
- [ ] **zero** /ˈziroʊ/ 零 it looked like nothing I had ever seen before
- [ ] **half** /hæf/ 半 half a loaf
- [ ] **dozen** /ˈdəzən/一打: So he wound up with a dozen.
- [x] **score** /skɔr/ 得分 she made good marks in algebra

- [ ] **second** /ˈsɛkənd/ 第二
- [ ] **third** /θərd/ 第三
- [ ] **fourth** /fɔrθ/第四: The Birds got five hits and all three of their runs off Kunkel before Hartman took over in the top of the fourth.
- [ ] **fifth** /fɪθ/第五: In the fifth, Wally Post slashed a 2-run homer off Bud Daley, but by that time the score was 11-5 and it really didn't matter.
- [ ] **sixth** /sɪksθ/ 第六
- [ ] **seventh** /ˈsɛvənθ/ 第七
- [ ] **eighth** /eɪtθ/ 第八
- [ ] **ninth** /naɪnθ/ 第九 going into the ninth they were a run ahead
- [ ] **tenth** /tɛnθ/ 第十
- [ ] **eleventh** /ɪˈlɛvənθ/ 第十一
- [ ] **twelfth** /twɛlfθ/第十二: It happened on the twelfth hole, a 155-yarder.
- [ ] **twentieth** /tˈwɛnˌtiɛθ/第二十: The specific instance I have in mind is the Afro-Asian version which has gained prominence only in this second half of the twentieth century.

## int. 感叹词

### exclamation 感叹

- [ ] **hi** /haɪ/ 嗨 every morning they exchanged polite hellos
- [ ] **god** /gɑd/天哪: -- and His exaltation to the right hand of God.
- [ ] **dear** /dɪr/亲爱的: `` Dear Doctors: We learned this year that our older son, Daniel, is autistic.
- [ ] **hello** /həˈloʊ/ 你好
- [ ] **cheers** /ʧɪrz/干杯: She was generous with her encores and the audience was equally so with its cheers and applause and flowers.
- [ ] **bye-bye** /ˈbaɪˈbaɪ/ 再见
- [ ] **good-bye** /ˈgʊdˌbaɪ/ 再见 they said their good-byes

## 说明


- [ ] 音标来自 eng\_to\_ipa
- [ ] 例句来自 nltk 或生成
- [ ] 如果要调整行的顺序，可以解析为列表操作，再写回。
- [ ] 可以多细分为很多层级。
- [ ] 一个单词可以有不同的词性，不同的意思。高频意思都需要。
- [ ] 复杂的单词可以用 中文（=...） 的形式标注简单的英文解释或者同义词。
- [ ] 每类中高频词往前，意思相近/反在一起，有特定顺序的按照特定顺序。
- [ ] 可以根据需要任意多层级，可多可少。
- [ ] 你觉得每个分类下面有没有遗漏应该属于这个分类的单词.
- [ ] 一个单词的同义词单词可以使用子list, 使用 \t 缩进。

## claude.md

**词条格式**

每条格式为：`- [ ] **单词** /音标/ pos. 中文释义（=简单英文释义）：例句`
- [ ] 带 `（=...）` 的简单英文释义标注用于复杂单词。

**编辑原则**

1. 高频词往前，同义词/反义词放一起。星期、月份、数字等有自然顺序，严格按序排列。
2. 同一个单词可以同时出现在不同词性或分类下。
